\ProblemFileHeader{500}
\ifquestionPull
\ifproblemToFind\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{x^{3} - 5}{x^{\frac{7}{2}}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{7 \, x^{\frac{5}{2}} - \frac{5}{\sqrt{x}}}{2 \, x^{4}} - \frac{4 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{2}} - 5 \, \sqrt{x}\right)}}{x^{5}}}$
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x + 4\right)} {\left(x - 1\right)}}{{\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 3\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 3\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{2 \, x + 3}{x^{\frac{2}{3}} - 9} - \frac{2 \, {\left(x^{2} + 3 \, x - 4\right)}}{3 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} {\left(x^{\frac{2}{3}} - 9\right)}^{2}}}$
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(\sqrt{x} - 2\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 4\right)}}{{\left(\sqrt{x} + 3\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} - 3\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{\frac{5}{x^{\frac{1}{6}}} + \frac{12}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{4}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}}{6 \, {\left(x - 9\right)}} - \frac{x^{\frac{5}{6}} + 4 \, \sqrt{x} - 2 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 8}{{\left(x - 9\right)}^{2}}}$
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{3} - 4\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} + 2\right)}}{{\left(x + 1\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} - 1\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{7 \, x^{\frac{5}{2}} + 12 \, x^{2} - \frac{4}{\sqrt{x}}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{3}{2}} - x + \sqrt{x} - 1\right)}} - \frac{{\left(x^{\frac{7}{2}} + 2 \, x^{3} - 4 \, \sqrt{x} - 8\right)} {\left(3 \, \sqrt{x} + \frac{1}{\sqrt{x}} - 2\right)}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{3}{2}} - x + \sqrt{x} - 1\right)}^{2}}}$
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{x^{\frac{1}{3}} {\left(\sqrt{x} - 1\right)}}{{\left(x + 5\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} - 5\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{{\left(x^{\frac{5}{6}} - x^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)} {\left(3 \, \sqrt{x} + \frac{5}{\sqrt{x}} - 10\right)}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{3}{2}} - 5 \, x + 5 \, \sqrt{x} - 25\right)}^{2}} + \frac{\frac{5}{x^{\frac{1}{6}}} - \frac{2}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}}{6 \, {\left(x^{\frac{3}{2}} - 5 \, x + 5 \, \sqrt{x} - 25\right)}}}$
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{2} - 2\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} + 3\right)}}{{\left(x + 5\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} - 5\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{5 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}} + 12 \, x - \frac{2}{\sqrt{x}}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{3}{2}} - 5 \, x + 5 \, \sqrt{x} - 25\right)}} - \frac{{\left(x^{\frac{5}{2}} + 3 \, x^{2} - 2 \, \sqrt{x} - 6\right)} {\left(3 \, \sqrt{x} + \frac{5}{\sqrt{x}} - 10\right)}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{3}{2}} - 5 \, x + 5 \, \sqrt{x} - 25\right)}^{2}}}$
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x - 5\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} + 4\right)}}{{\left(x^{3} + 4\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 4\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{2 \, {\left(5 \, x^{\frac{7}{3}} - 18 \, x^{2} + \frac{2}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{3}{2}} + 4 \, x - 5 \, \sqrt{x} - 20\right)}}{3 \, {\left(x^{\frac{10}{3}} - 4 \, x^{3} + 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 16\right)}^{2}} + \frac{3 \, \sqrt{x} - \frac{5}{\sqrt{x}} + 8}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{10}{3}} - 4 \, x^{3} + 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 16\right)}}}$
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{2} + 3\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} + 5\right)}}{{\left(x - 1\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} + 1\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{5 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}} + 20 \, x + \frac{3}{\sqrt{x}}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{3}{2}} + x - \sqrt{x} - 1\right)}} - \frac{{\left(x^{\frac{5}{2}} + 5 \, x^{2} + 3 \, \sqrt{x} + 15\right)} {\left(3 \, \sqrt{x} - \frac{1}{\sqrt{x}} + 2\right)}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{3}{2}} + x - \sqrt{x} - 1\right)}^{2}}}$
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x + 5\right)} {\left(x - 1\right)}}{{\left(x^{2} - 4\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} + 4\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{{\left(x^{2} + 4 \, x - 5\right)} {\left(5 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}} + 16 \, x - \frac{4}{\sqrt{x}}\right)}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{5}{2}} + 4 \, x^{2} - 4 \, \sqrt{x} - 16\right)}^{2}} + \frac{2 \, {\left(x + 2\right)}}{x^{\frac{5}{2}} + 4 \, x^{2} - 4 \, \sqrt{x} - 16}}$
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{3} - 5\right)} x^{3}}{{\left(x^{2} + 4\right)} {\left(x^{2} - 4\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{4 \, {\left(x^{6} - 5 \, x^{3}\right)} x^{3}}{{\left(x^{4} - 16\right)}^{2}} + \frac{3 \, {\left(2 \, x^{5} - 5 \, x^{2}\right)}}{x^{4} - 16}}$
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{3} - 4\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} - 5\right)}}{{\left(x^{2} + 2\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 2\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{7 \, x^{\frac{5}{2}} - 30 \, x^{2} - \frac{4}{\sqrt{x}}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{3}} - 2 \, x^{2} + 2 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 4\right)}} - \frac{{\left(x^{\frac{7}{2}} - 5 \, x^{3} - 4 \, \sqrt{x} + 20\right)} {\left(7 \, x^{\frac{4}{3}} - 12 \, x + \frac{2}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}\right)}}{3 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{3}} - 2 \, x^{2} + 2 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 4\right)}^{2}}}$
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(\sqrt{x} - 1\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 5\right)}}{{\left(\sqrt{x} - 4\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 4\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{{\left(x^{\frac{5}{6}} - 5 \, \sqrt{x} - x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 5\right)} {\left(\frac{5}{x^{\frac{1}{6}}} + \frac{12}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{8}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}\right)}}{6 \, {\left(x^{\frac{5}{6}} + 4 \, \sqrt{x} - 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 16\right)}^{2}} + \frac{\frac{5}{x^{\frac{1}{6}}} - \frac{15}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{2}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}}{6 \, {\left(x^{\frac{5}{6}} + 4 \, \sqrt{x} - 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 16\right)}}}$
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{2} + 3\right)} x}{{\left(x^{3} + 2\right)} {\left(x - 2\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{2 \, {\left(2 \, x^{3} - 3 \, x^{2} + 1\right)} {\left(x^{3} + 3 \, x\right)}}{{\left(x^{4} - 2 \, x^{3} + 2 \, x - 4\right)}^{2}} + \frac{3 \, {\left(x^{2} + 1\right)}}{x^{4} - 2 \, x^{3} + 2 \, x - 4}}$
\end{problem}}

\latexProblemContent{

\begin{problem}

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x + 5\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 2\right)}}{{\left(x^{2} + 2\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} - 2\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{{\left(5 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}} - 8 \, x + \frac{2}{\sqrt{x}}\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{4}{3}} + 2 \, x + 5 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 10\right)}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{5}{2}} - 2 \, x^{2} + 2 \, \sqrt{x} - 4\right)}^{2}} + \frac{4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} + \frac{5}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}} + 6}{3 \, {\left(x^{\frac{5}{2}} - 2 \, x^{2} + 2 \, \sqrt{x} - 4\right)}}}$
\end{problem}}

\latexProblemContent{

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{3} + 4\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 5\right)}}{x^{\frac{4}{3}}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{10 \, x^{\frac{7}{3}} - 45 \, x^{2} + \frac{4}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}}{3 \, x^{\frac{4}{3}}} - \frac{4 \, {\left(x^{\frac{10}{3}} - 5 \, x^{3} + 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 20\right)}}{3 \, x^{\frac{7}{3}}}}$
\end{problem}}

\latexProblemContent{

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{{\left(5 \, x^{4} + 9 \, x^{2} - 6 \, x\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{7}{2}} - 4 \, x^{3} - 2 \, \sqrt{x} + 8\right)}}{{\left(x^{5} + 3 \, x^{3} - 3 \, x^{2} - 9\right)}^{2}} + \frac{7 \, x^{\frac{5}{2}} - 24 \, x^{2} - \frac{2}{\sqrt{x}}}{2 \, {\left(x^{5} + 3 \, x^{3} - 3 \, x^{2} - 9\right)}}}$
\end{problem}}

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{{\left(5 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}} - 16 \, x + \frac{4}{\sqrt{x}}\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{5}{6}} + 4 \, \sqrt{x} - x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 4\right)}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{5}{2}} - 4 \, x^{2} + 4 \, \sqrt{x} - 16\right)}^{2}} + \frac{\frac{5}{x^{\frac{1}{6}}} + \frac{12}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{2}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}}{6 \, {\left(x^{\frac{5}{2}} - 4 \, x^{2} + 4 \, \sqrt{x} - 16\right)}}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{\frac{5}{x^{\frac{1}{6}}} - \frac{3}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{4}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}}{6 \, x^{5}} - \frac{5 \, {\left(x^{\frac{5}{6}} - \sqrt{x} - 2 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 2\right)}}{x^{6}}}$
\end{problem}}

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{7 \, x^{\frac{5}{2}} - 18 \, x^{2} + \frac{1}{\sqrt{x}}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{10}{3}} - 4 \, x^{3} + 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 16\right)}} - \frac{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{2}} - 3 \, x^{3} + \sqrt{x} - 3\right)} {\left(5 \, x^{\frac{7}{3}} - 18 \, x^{2} + \frac{2}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}\right)}}{3 \, {\left(x^{\frac{10}{3}} - 4 \, x^{3} + 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 16\right)}^{2}}}$

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{2} - 3\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} + 1\right)}}{{\left(x^{3} + 5\right)} {\left(x^{3} - 5\right)}}$

\end{problem}}

\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x + 2\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 3\right)}}{{\left(x^{2} + 5\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 5\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{{\left(7 \, x^{\frac{4}{3}} - 30 \, x + \frac{5}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{4}{3}} + 3 \, x + 2 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 6\right)}}{3 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{3}} - 5 \, x^{2} + 5 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 25\right)}^{2}} + \frac{4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} + \frac{2}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}} + 9}{3 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{3}} - 5 \, x^{2} + 5 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 25\right)}}}$
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 4}{x^{\frac{7}{2}}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{\frac{5}{x^{\frac{1}{6}}} - \frac{12}{\sqrt{x}}}{6 \, x^{4}} - \frac{4 \, {\left(x^{\frac{5}{6}} - 4 \, \sqrt{x}\right)}}{x^{5}}}$
\end{problem}}

\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{2} - 2\right)} {\left(x^{2} - 3\right)}}{x^{\frac{5}{6}}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{2 \, {\left(2 \, x^{3} - 5 \, x\right)}}{x^{\frac{5}{6}}} - \frac{5 \, {\left(x^{4} - 5 \, x^{2} + 6\right)}}{6 \, x^{\frac{11}{6}}}}$
\end{problem}}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{2} + 5\right)} {\left(x^{2} + 2\right)}}{{\left(\sqrt{x} - 4\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 4\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{2 \, {\left(2 \, x^{3} + 7 \, x\right)}}{x^{\frac{5}{6}} + 4 \, \sqrt{x} - 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 16} - \frac{{\left(x^{4} + 7 \, x^{2} + 10\right)} {\left(\frac{5}{x^{\frac{1}{6}}} + \frac{12}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{8}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}\right)}}{6 \, {\left(x^{\frac{5}{6}} + 4 \, \sqrt{x} - 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 16\right)}^{2}}}$
\end{problem}}

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{{\left(7 \, x^{\frac{5}{2}} - 24 \, x^{2} + \frac{4}{\sqrt{x}}\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{7}{3}} - x^{2} - 2 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 2\right)}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{2}} - 4 \, x^{3} + 4 \, \sqrt{x} - 16\right)}^{2}} + \frac{7 \, x^{\frac{4}{3}} - 6 \, x - \frac{2}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}}{3 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{2}} - 4 \, x^{3} + 4 \, \sqrt{x} - 16\right)}}}$

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{{\left(x^{\frac{2}{3}} - 5 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 6\right)} {\left(3 \, \sqrt{x} + \frac{2}{\sqrt{x}} - 4\right)}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{3}{2}} - 2 \, x + 2 \, \sqrt{x} - 4\right)}^{2}} + \frac{\frac{2}{x^{\frac{1}{3}}} - \frac{5}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}}{3 \, {\left(x^{\frac{3}{2}} - 2 \, x + 2 \, \sqrt{x} - 4\right)}}}$

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{2} + 2\right)} {\left(x - 1\right)}}{{\left(\sqrt{x} + 4\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} - 4\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{3 \, x^{2} - 2 \, x + 2}{x - 16} - \frac{x^{3} - x^{2} + 2 \, x - 2}{{\left(x - 16\right)}^{2}}}$
\end{problem}}

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{5 \, x^{4} + 9 \, x^{2} + 4 \, x}{x^{\frac{7}{3}} + 3 \, x^{2} - 3 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 9} - \frac{{\left(x^{5} + 3 \, x^{3} + 2 \, x^{2} + 6\right)} {\left(7 \, x^{\frac{4}{3}} + 18 \, x - \frac{3}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}\right)}}{3 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{3}} + 3 \, x^{2} - 3 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 9\right)}^{2}}}$
\end{problem}}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(\sqrt{x} - 3\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 3\right)}}{{\left(x - 5\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} + 5\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{{\left(x^{\frac{5}{6}} + 3 \, \sqrt{x} - 3 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 9\right)} {\left(3 \, \sqrt{x} - \frac{5}{\sqrt{x}} + 10\right)}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{3}{2}} + 5 \, x - 5 \, \sqrt{x} - 25\right)}^{2}} + \frac{\frac{5}{x^{\frac{1}{6}}} + \frac{9}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{6}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}}{6 \, {\left(x^{\frac{3}{2}} + 5 \, x - 5 \, \sqrt{x} - 25\right)}}}$
\end{problem}}

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{2} + 5\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 4\right)}}{{\left(x^{3} + 5\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} - 5\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{{\left(7 \, x^{\frac{5}{2}} - 30 \, x^{2} + \frac{5}{\sqrt{x}}\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{7}{3}} + 4 \, x^{2} + 5 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 20\right)}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{2}} - 5 \, x^{3} + 5 \, \sqrt{x} - 25\right)}^{2}} + \frac{7 \, x^{\frac{4}{3}} + 24 \, x + \frac{5}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}}{3 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{2}} - 5 \, x^{3} + 5 \, \sqrt{x} - 25\right)}}}$
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{2} - 2\right)}^{2}}{{\left(x^{2} + 2\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} - 2\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{4 \, {\left(x^{3} - 2 \, x\right)}}{x^{\frac{5}{2}} - 2 \, x^{2} + 2 \, \sqrt{x} - 4} - \frac{{\left(x^{4} - 4 \, x^{2} + 4\right)} {\left(5 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}} - 8 \, x + \frac{2}{\sqrt{x}}\right)}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{5}{2}} - 2 \, x^{2} + 2 \, \sqrt{x} - 4\right)}^{2}}}$
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(\sqrt{x} - 3\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 4\right)}}{{\left(x^{3} - 5\right)} {\left(x + 5\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{{\left(4 \, x^{3} + 15 \, x^{2} - 5\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{5}{6}} - 4 \, \sqrt{x} - 3 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 12\right)}}{{\left(x^{4} + 5 \, x^{3} - 5 \, x - 25\right)}^{2}} + \frac{\frac{5}{x^{\frac{1}{6}}} - \frac{12}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{6}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}}{6 \, {\left(x^{4} + 5 \, x^{3} - 5 \, x - 25\right)}}}$
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{2} - 1\right)} {\left(x - 5\right)}}{{\left(\sqrt{x} + 4\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 4\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{3 \, x^{2} - 10 \, x - 1}{x^{\frac{5}{6}} - 4 \, \sqrt{x} + 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 16} - \frac{{\left(x^{3} - 5 \, x^{2} - x + 5\right)} {\left(\frac{5}{x^{\frac{1}{6}}} - \frac{12}{\sqrt{x}} + \frac{8}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}\right)}}{6 \, {\left(x^{\frac{5}{6}} - 4 \, \sqrt{x} + 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 16\right)}^{2}}}$
\end{problem}}

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{x^{3} + 4}{\sqrt{x} - 3}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{3 \, {\left(2 \, x^{5} + 7 \, x^{2}\right)}}{x^{\frac{7}{2}} - 3 \, x^{3} + 3 \, \sqrt{x} - 9} - \frac{{\left(x^{6} + 7 \, x^{3} + 12\right)} {\left(7 \, x^{\frac{5}{2}} - 18 \, x^{2} + \frac{3}{\sqrt{x}}\right)}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{2}} - 3 \, x^{3} + 3 \, \sqrt{x} - 9\right)}^{2}}}$
\end{problem}}

\begin{problem}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{3} - 5\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} + 4\right)}}{{\left(x^{2} - 5\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 5\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{7 \, x^{\frac{5}{2}} + 24 \, x^{2} - \frac{5}{\sqrt{x}}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{3}} + 5 \, x^{2} - 5 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 25\right)}} - \frac{{\left(x^{\frac{7}{2}} + 4 \, x^{3} - 5 \, \sqrt{x} - 20\right)} {\left(7 \, x^{\frac{4}{3}} + 30 \, x - \frac{5}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}\right)}}{3 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{3}} + 5 \, x^{2} - 5 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 25\right)}^{2}}}$
\end{problem}}

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{2}} + x^{3} - \sqrt{x} - 1\right)} {\left(2 \, x^{3} + 3 \, x^{2} - 1\right)}}{{\left(x^{4} + 2 \, x^{3} - 2 \, x - 4\right)}^{2}} + \frac{7 \, x^{\frac{5}{2}} + 6 \, x^{2} - \frac{1}{\sqrt{x}}}{2 \, {\left(x^{4} + 2 \, x^{3} - 2 \, x - 4\right)}}}$
\end{problem}}

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x + 3\right)} {\left(x - 1\right)}}{{\left(x^{2} - 2\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} + 2\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{{\left(x^{2} + 2 \, x - 3\right)} {\left(5 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}} + 8 \, x - \frac{2}{\sqrt{x}}\right)}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{5}{2}} + 2 \, x^{2} - 2 \, \sqrt{x} - 4\right)}^{2}} + \frac{2 \, {\left(x + 1\right)}}{x^{\frac{5}{2}} + 2 \, x^{2} - 2 \, \sqrt{x} - 4}}$
\end{problem}}

\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{3} - 3\right)} {\left(x^{2} - 3\right)}}{{\left(x^{2} - 2\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 2\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{5 \, x^{4} - 9 \, x^{2} - 6 \, x}{x^{\frac{7}{3}} + 2 \, x^{2} - 2 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 4} - \frac{{\left(x^{5} - 3 \, x^{3} - 3 \, x^{2} + 9\right)} {\left(7 \, x^{\frac{4}{3}} + 12 \, x - \frac{2}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}\right)}}{3 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{3}} + 2 \, x^{2} - 2 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 4\right)}^{2}}}$
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{3} + 3\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} + 3\right)}}{x^{6}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{7 \, x^{\frac{5}{2}} + 18 \, x^{2} + \frac{3}{\sqrt{x}}}{2 \, x^{6}} - \frac{6 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{2}} + 3 \, x^{3} + 3 \, \sqrt{x} + 9\right)}}{x^{7}}}$
\end{problem}}

\end{problem}}

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{3} - 2\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 2\right)}}{{\left(\sqrt{x} - 3\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 3\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{2 \, {\left(5 \, x^{\frac{7}{3}} + 9 \, x^{2} - \frac{1}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}\right)}}{3 \, {\left(x^{\frac{5}{6}} + 3 \, \sqrt{x} - 3 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 9\right)}} - \frac{{\left(x^{\frac{10}{3}} + 2 \, x^{3} - 2 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 4\right)} {\left(\frac{5}{x^{\frac{1}{6}}} + \frac{9}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{6}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}\right)}}{6 \, {\left(x^{\frac{5}{6}} + 3 \, \sqrt{x} - 3 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 9\right)}^{2}}}$
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{2} - 3\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} - 4\right)}}{x^{4}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{5 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}} - 16 \, x - \frac{3}{\sqrt{x}}}{2 \, x^{4}} - \frac{4 \, {\left(x^{\frac{5}{2}} - 4 \, x^{2} - 3 \, \sqrt{x} + 12\right)}}{x^{5}}}$
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{2} - 3\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 5\right)}}{{\left(x + 4\right)} {\left(x - 4\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{7 \, x^{\frac{4}{3}} + 30 \, x - \frac{3}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}}{3 \, {\left(x^{2} - 16\right)}} - \frac{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{3}} + 5 \, x^{2} - 3 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 15\right)} x}{{\left(x^{2} - 16\right)}^{2}}}$
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{x^{2} {\left(\sqrt{x} + 1\right)}}{{\left(x^{3} + 4\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 4\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{5}{2}} + x^{2}\right)} {\left(5 \, x^{\frac{7}{3}} - 18 \, x^{2} + \frac{2}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}\right)}}{3 \, {\left(x^{\frac{10}{3}} - 4 \, x^{3} + 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 16\right)}^{2}} + \frac{5 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}} + 4 \, x}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{10}{3}} - 4 \, x^{3} + 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 16\right)}}}$
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{3} - 4\right)} {\left(x - 2\right)}}{{\left(x^{3} + 5\right)} {\left(x - 5\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{{\left(x^{4} - 2 \, x^{3} - 4 \, x + 8\right)} {\left(4 \, x^{3} - 15 \, x^{2} + 5\right)}}{{\left(x^{4} - 5 \, x^{3} + 5 \, x - 25\right)}^{2}} + \frac{2 \, {\left(2 \, x^{3} - 3 \, x^{2} - 2\right)}}{x^{4} - 5 \, x^{3} + 5 \, x - 25}}$
\end{problem}}

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(\sqrt{x} - 3\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 1\right)}}{{\left(x^{2} - 5\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} + 5\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{5 \, {\left(x^{\frac{3}{2}} + 4 \, x - \frac{1}{\sqrt{x}}\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{5}{6}} - \sqrt{x} - 3 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 3\right)}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{5}{2}} + 5 \, x^{2} - 5 \, \sqrt{x} - 25\right)}^{2}} + \frac{\frac{5}{x^{\frac{1}{6}}} - \frac{3}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{6}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}}{6 \, {\left(x^{\frac{5}{2}} + 5 \, x^{2} - 5 \, \sqrt{x} - 25\right)}}}$
\end{problem}}

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{2 \, {\left(5 \, x^{\frac{7}{3}} + 18 \, x^{2} - \frac{2}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{3}{2}} - x + 5 \, \sqrt{x} - 5\right)}}{3 \, {\left(x^{\frac{10}{3}} + 4 \, x^{3} - 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 16\right)}^{2}} + \frac{3 \, \sqrt{x} + \frac{5}{\sqrt{x}} - 2}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{10}{3}} + 4 \, x^{3} - 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 16\right)}}}$
\end{problem}}

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

\end{problem}}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{2} + 3\right)} {\left(x^{2} + 1\right)}}{{\left(x^{3} - 1\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} + 1\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{4 \, {\left(x^{3} + 2 \, x\right)}}{x^{\frac{7}{2}} + x^{3} - \sqrt{x} - 1} - \frac{{\left(x^{4} + 4 \, x^{2} + 3\right)} {\left(7 \, x^{\frac{5}{2}} + 6 \, x^{2} - \frac{1}{\sqrt{x}}\right)}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{2}} + x^{3} - \sqrt{x} - 1\right)}^{2}}}$
\end{problem}}

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{3 \, {\left(2 \, x^{5} - 3 \, x^{2}\right)}}{x^{\frac{10}{3}} + 3 \, x^{3} - 3 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 9} - \frac{{\left(x^{6} - 3 \, x^{3} - 4\right)} {\left(10 \, x^{\frac{7}{3}} + 27 \, x^{2} - \frac{3}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}\right)}}{3 \, {\left(x^{\frac{10}{3}} + 3 \, x^{3} - 3 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 9\right)}^{2}}}$

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{2} + 1\right)} x^{2}}{{\left(x^{3} + 4\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 4\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{2 \, {\left(2 \, x^{3} + x\right)}}{x^{\frac{10}{3}} - 4 \, x^{3} + 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 16} - \frac{2 \, {\left(x^{4} + x^{2}\right)} {\left(5 \, x^{\frac{7}{3}} - 18 \, x^{2} + \frac{2}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}\right)}}{3 \, {\left(x^{\frac{10}{3}} - 4 \, x^{3} + 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 16\right)}^{2}}}$
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(\sqrt{x} + 3\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 2\right)}}{{\left(x^{3} + 1\right)} {\left(x - 1\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{{\left(4 \, x^{3} - 3 \, x^{2} + 1\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{5}{6}} + 2 \, \sqrt{x} + 3 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 6\right)}}{{\left(x^{4} - x^{3} + x - 1\right)}^{2}} + \frac{\frac{5}{x^{\frac{1}{6}}} + \frac{6}{\sqrt{x}} + \frac{6}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}}{6 \, {\left(x^{4} - x^{3} + x - 1\right)}}}$
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(\sqrt{x} - 5\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 4\right)}}{{\left(x + 5\right)} {\left(x - 5\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{2 \, x {\left(x^{\frac{5}{6}} - 4 \, \sqrt{x} - 5 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 20\right)}}{{\left(x^{2} - 25\right)}^{2}} + \frac{\frac{5}{x^{\frac{1}{6}}} - \frac{12}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{10}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}}{6 \, {\left(x^{2} - 25\right)}}}$
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{2} - 2\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} + 5\right)}}{{\left(x^{3} + 2\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} - 2\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{{\left(7 \, x^{\frac{5}{2}} - 12 \, x^{2} + \frac{2}{\sqrt{x}}\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{5}{2}} + 5 \, x^{2} - 2 \, \sqrt{x} - 10\right)}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{2}} - 2 \, x^{3} + 2 \, \sqrt{x} - 4\right)}^{2}} + \frac{5 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}} + 20 \, x - \frac{2}{\sqrt{x}}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{2}} - 2 \, x^{3} + 2 \, \sqrt{x} - 4\right)}}}$
\end{problem}}

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x - 5\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 1\right)}}{{\left(x^{2} - 4\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 4\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{{\left(7 \, x^{\frac{4}{3}} + 24 \, x - \frac{4}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{4}{3}} + x - 5 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 5\right)}}{3 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{3}} + 4 \, x^{2} - 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 16\right)}^{2}} + \frac{4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - \frac{5}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}} + 3}{3 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{3}} + 4 \, x^{2} - 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 16\right)}}}$
\end{problem}}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{2} - 4\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 1\right)}}{{\left(\sqrt{x} + 1\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} - 1\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{7 \, x^{\frac{4}{3}} - 6 \, x - \frac{4}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}}{3 \, {\left(x - 1\right)}} - \frac{x^{\frac{7}{3}} - x^{2} - 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 4}{{\left(x - 1\right)}^{2}}}$
\end{problem}}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x + 3\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 1\right)}}{{\left(x^{2} + 4\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 4\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{{\left(7 \, x^{\frac{4}{3}} - 24 \, x + \frac{4}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{4}{3}} + x + 3 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 3\right)}}{3 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{3}} - 4 \, x^{2} + 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 16\right)}^{2}} + \frac{4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} + \frac{3}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}} + 3}{3 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{3}} - 4 \, x^{2} + 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 16\right)}}}$
\end{problem}}

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{2} + 2\right)} {\left(x + 2\right)}}{{\left(x^{3} - 2\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 2\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{2 \, {\left(x^{3} + 2 \, x^{2} + 2 \, x + 4\right)} {\left(5 \, x^{\frac{7}{3}} + 9 \, x^{2} - \frac{1}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}\right)}}{3 \, {\left(x^{\frac{10}{3}} + 2 \, x^{3} - 2 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 4\right)}^{2}} + \frac{3 \, x^{2} + 4 \, x + 2}{x^{\frac{10}{3}} + 2 \, x^{3} - 2 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 4}}$
\end{problem}}

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{4 \, {\left(x^{\frac{4}{3}} + 4 \, x + 3 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} + 12\right)} x^{3}}{{\left(x^{4} - 4\right)}^{2}} + \frac{4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} + \frac{3}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}} + 12}{3 \, {\left(x^{4} - 4\right)}}}$
\end{problem}}

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{2 \, {\left(5 \, x^{\frac{7}{3}} + 18 \, x^{2} - \frac{2}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{5}{6}} + \sqrt{x} - x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 1\right)}}{3 \, {\left(x^{\frac{10}{3}} + 4 \, x^{3} - 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 16\right)}^{2}} + \frac{\frac{5}{x^{\frac{1}{6}}} + \frac{3}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{2}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}}{6 \, {\left(x^{\frac{10}{3}} + 4 \, x^{3} - 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 16\right)}}}$

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{3} + 3\right)} {\left(x^{2} + 5\right)}}{{\left(x^{2} + 4\right)} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 4\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{5 \, x^{4} + 15 \, x^{2} + 6 \, x}{x^{\frac{7}{3}} - 4 \, x^{2} + 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 16} - \frac{{\left(x^{5} + 5 \, x^{3} + 3 \, x^{2} + 15\right)} {\left(7 \, x^{\frac{4}{3}} - 24 \, x + \frac{4}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}\right)}}{3 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{3}} - 4 \, x^{2} + 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 16\right)}^{2}}}$
\end{problem}}

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{5 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}} + 20 \, x - \frac{2}{\sqrt{x}}}{2 \, {\left(x - 9\right)}} - \frac{x^{\frac{5}{2}} + 5 \, x^{2} - 2 \, \sqrt{x} - 10}{{\left(x - 9\right)}^{2}}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{6 \, {\left(x^{4} + 5 \, x^{3} - 3 \, x - 15\right)} x^{5}}{{\left(x^{6} - 4\right)}^{2}} + \frac{4 \, x^{3} + 15 \, x^{2} - 3}{x^{6} - 4}}$
\end{problem}}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{x^{\frac{1}{3}} {\left(x^{\frac{1}{3}} - 4\right)}}{{\left(x - 4\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} + 4\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{{\left(x^{\frac{2}{3}} - 4 \, x^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)} {\left(3 \, \sqrt{x} - \frac{4}{\sqrt{x}} + 8\right)}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{3}{2}} + 4 \, x - 4 \, \sqrt{x} - 16\right)}^{2}} + \frac{2 \, {\left(\frac{1}{x^{\frac{1}{3}}} - \frac{2}{x^{\frac{2}{3}}}\right)}}{3 \, {\left(x^{\frac{3}{2}} + 4 \, x - 4 \, \sqrt{x} - 16\right)}}}$
\end{problem}}

\latexProblemContent{

\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = \frac{{\left(x^{3} - 4\right)} {\left(x^{2} - 4\right)}}{{\left(x + 3\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} - 3\right)}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{5 \, x^{4} - 12 \, x^{2} - 8 \, x}{x^{\frac{3}{2}} - 3 \, x + 3 \, \sqrt{x} - 9} - \frac{3 \, {\left(x^{5} - 4 \, x^{3} - 4 \, x^{2} + 16\right)} {\left(\sqrt{x} + \frac{1}{\sqrt{x}} - 2\right)}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{3}{2}} - 3 \, x + 3 \, \sqrt{x} - 9\right)}^{2}}}$
\end{problem}}

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{6 \, {\left(x^{5} - x^{2}\right)}}{x^{\frac{7}{2}} + x^{3} - \sqrt{x} - 1} - \frac{{\left(x^{6} - 2 \, x^{3} - 8\right)} {\left(7 \, x^{\frac{5}{2}} + 6 \, x^{2} - \frac{1}{\sqrt{x}}\right)}}{2 \, {\left(x^{\frac{7}{2}} + x^{3} - \sqrt{x} - 1\right)}^{2}}}$

\begin{problem}

$f'(x) = \answer{\frac{3 \, \sqrt{x} - \frac{5}{\sqrt{x}} - 2}{2 \, x^{4}} - \frac{4 \, {\left(x^{\frac{3}{2}} - x - 5 \, \sqrt{x} + 5\right)}}{x^{5}}}$
\end{problem}}
